        256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1)
        (activation): ReLU()
      )
      (deconv): ConvTranspose2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(2, 2), stride=(2, 2))
      (deconv_relu): ReLU()
      (predictor): Conv2d(256, 4, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
    )
  )
)
